### Development Step 7: Identify Berlin Football Club Winning 1984 DDR-Pokal and Its October 2, 1985 European Match

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify the Berlin-based football club that won the last East German Cup in 1984. Search for keywords including 'East German Cup 1984 winner Berlin football club', 'DDR-Pokal 1984 final Berlin team', 'last East German Cup 1984 champion', and 'GDR Cup 1984 Berlin football'. Focus on identifying which Berlin club won this final East German Cup tournament and gather information about their European competition participation in the 1985-86 season, particularly any matches on 2 October 1985.

**Use Cases**:
- Sports historians automating the retrieval of archived match reports and statistics for museum exhibitions on East German football
- Investigative sports journalists verifying specific game dates, opponents, and venues to fact-check feature articles on BFC Dynamo’s European campaigns
- Football fan sites populating their club history pages with accurate details from the 1985-86 UEFA Cup Winners’ Cup using targeted web searches
- Documentary researchers compiling precise timelines and contextual snippets for a film on DDR-era football through multi-query API extraction
- Academic sports scientists aggregating performance data of East German clubs in European competitions for statistical trend analysis
- Data engineers building a structured historical sports database by systematically querying and filtering online sources for exact match information
- Educators designing interactive quizzes and lesson plans on German football history, automatically sourcing validated match outcomes and dates
- Mobile app developers integrating a dynamic timeline feature that auto-loads historical match events (e.g., 2 October 1985) for fan engagement tools

```
import os
import requests
import json
from datetime import datetime

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print("API key found, proceeding with targeted search for BFC Dynamo's 2 October 1985 European match...")
print("Based on previous analysis: BFC Dynamo was Berlin finalist in 1984 East German Cup (lost to Dresden)")
print("Target: Find specific European competition match on 2 October 1985")
print("=" * 80)

# Define targeted search queries for BFC Dynamo's 2 October 1985 European match
search_queries = [
'BFC Dynamo "2 October 1985" European competition match',
'Berliner FC Dynamo "October 2 1985" UEFA Cup Winners Cup',
'BFC Dynamo European match "2.10.1985" opponent venue',
'Berliner FC Dynamo "2nd October 1985" European football',
'BFC Dynamo 1985-86 European season "October 2" match report',
'East German BFC Dynamo "2 October 1985" European Cup',
'Dynamo Berlin "2.10.85" European competition result',
'BFC Dynamo 1985 European matches October 2nd opponent'
]

print(f"Starting targeted search with {len(search_queries)} specific queries...")
print("Focus: BFC Dynamo European match on exactly 2 October 1985")
print("=" * 80)

# Store all search results for analysis
all_results = []
successful_searches = 0
failed_searches = 0

# Perform searches with different targeted queries
for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}")
print("-" * 70)

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 10, # Get sufficient results for comprehensive analysis
"type": "search"
}

try:
# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()

if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results for search {i}")
successful_searches += 1

# Process and display key results
for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {j}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"Link: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Store result with search context
all_results.append({
'search_number': i,
'query_text': query,
'result_number': j,
'title': title,
'link': link,
'snippet': snippet
})

# Highlight potentially relevant results
combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}"
key_indicators = ['bfc dynamo', 'berliner fc dynamo', '2 october', 'october 2', '2.10.1985', 'european', 'uefa', 'cup winners']
matching_indicators = []
for term in key_indicators:
if term in combined_text:
matching_indicators.append(term)

if len(matching_indicators) >= 2:
print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}")

# Check for specific match details
if '2 october' in combined_text or 'october 2' in combined_text or '2.10.1985' in combined_text:
print(f"🗓️ EXACT DATE MATCH: Contains 2 October 1985 reference")
if 'opponent' in combined_text or 'vs' in combined_text or 'against' in combined_text:
print(f"⚽ MATCH DETAILS: Contains opponent information")
if 'venue' in combined_text or 'stadium' in combined_text:
print(f"🏟️ VENUE INFO: Contains stadium/venue details")

print("-" * 40)
else:
print(f"No organic results found for search {i}: '{query}'")
failed_searches += 1
all_results.append({
'search_number': i,
'query_text': query,
'result_number': 0,
'title': 'No results',
'link': 'N/A',
'snippet': 'No results found for this query'
})

else:
print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
failed_searches += 1

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}")
failed_searches += 1
continue

print("\n" + "=" * 80)

# Save comprehensive search results to workspace
timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
results_file = f"workspace/bfc_dynamo_2_october_1985_search_results_{timestamp}.json"

with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump({
'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
'search_purpose': 'BFC Dynamo European match on 2 October 1985 - targeted search',
'background_context': 'BFC Dynamo was Berlin finalist in 1984 East German Cup (lost to Dresden), regular European participant',
'total_queries': len(search_queries),
'successful_searches': successful_searches,
'failed_searches': failed_searches,
'total_results': len(all_results),
'queries_executed': search_queries,
'results': all_results
}, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"\n\n📊 TARGETED SEARCH SUMMARY:")
print(f"Total targeted queries executed: {len(search_queries)}")
print(f"Successful searches: {successful_searches}")
print(f"Failed searches: {failed_searches}")
print(f"Total results collected: {len(all_results)}")
print(f"Search results saved to: {results_file}")

# Quick analysis for immediate insights
print("\n\n🔍 QUICK ANALYSIS FOR 2 OCTOBER 1985 MATCH:")
print("=" * 60)

# Look for results specifically mentioning the exact date
exact_date_results = []
european_match_results = []
bfc_dynamo_results = []

for result in all_results:
if result['title'] == 'No results':
continue

title_lower = result['title'].lower()
snippet_lower = result['snippet'].lower()
combined = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}"

# Categorize by relevance to our specific search
if '2 october' in combined or 'october 2' in combined or '2.10.1985' in combined or '2.10.85' in combined:
exact_date_results.append(result)

if any(term in combined for term in ['european', 'uefa', 'cup winners', 'european cup']) and ('bfc dynamo' in combined or 'berliner fc dynamo' in combined):
european_match_results.append(result)

if 'bfc dynamo' in combined or 'berliner fc dynamo' in combined:
bfc_dynamo_results.append(result)

print(f"\n📋 QUICK CATEGORIZATION:")
print(f"Results with exact date (2 October 1985): {len(exact_date_results)}")
print(f"Results with BFC Dynamo European matches: {len(european_match_results)}")
print(f"Results mentioning BFC Dynamo: {len(bfc_dynamo_results)}")

# Display most promising results
if exact_date_results:
print("\n\n🎯 EXACT DATE MATCHES (2 October 1985):")
print("=" * 50)
for i, result in enumerate(exact_date_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3
print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}")
print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}")
print(f" Link: {result['link']}")
print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}")
print(f" Search #{result['search_number']}, Result #{result['result_number']}")
else:
print("\n⚠️ No exact date matches found for 2 October 1985")

if european_match_results:
print("\n\n🌍 BFC DYNAMO EUROPEAN COMPETITION RESULTS:")
print("=" * 50)
for i, result in enumerate(european_match_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3
print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}")
print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}")
print(f" Link: {result['link']}")
print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}")
else:
print("\n⚠️ No specific BFC Dynamo European match results found")

print(f"\n\n📁 Next step: Analyze detailed results in {results_file}")
print("🎯 Goal: Identify BFC Dynamo's specific European match on 2 October 1985")
print("🔍 Focus: Match opponent, venue, competition, and result details")
print("\n🏁 Targeted search phase complete - ready for detailed analysis!")
```

### Development Step 3: Identify Berlin club winning 1984 East German Cup and its 1985–86 European fixtures

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify the Berlin-based football club that won the last East German Cup in 1984. Search for keywords including 'East German Cup 1984 winner Berlin football club', 'DDR-Pokal 1984 final Berlin team', 'last East German Cup 1984 champion', and 'GDR Cup 1984 Berlin football'. Focus on identifying which Berlin club won this final East German Cup tournament and gather information about their European competition participation in the 1985-86 season, particularly any matches on 2 October 1985.

**Use Cases**:
- Historical sports research: automated web queries, snippet parsing, and summary report generation to document the outcomes and finalists of archival football tournaments
- Journalistic fact-checking: systematic retrieval and categorization of web search results to verify claims about past sports events and provide concise evidence summaries
- Academic literature review: automated searches across digital archives, categorization of relevant publications, and generation of structured analysis for a research paper on regional competitions
- Market intelligence reporting: scraping competitor press releases and news articles on product launches, categorizing by relevance, and exporting a summarized intelligence dossier
- Legal precedent analysis: conducting keyword-based web searches on case law, parsing snippets for verdict mentions, categorizing results by relevance, and producing a concise case summary file
- Brand sentiment monitoring: automated searches for online mentions of a brand, categorization of positive and negative snippets, and compilation of a sentiment analysis report
- Compliance audit automation: retrieving regulatory documents and news items, filtering by jurisdiction and topic, and summarizing critical compliance evidence for audit reviewers
- Event logistics planning: gathering venue availability, date confirmations, and attendance data for upcoming conferences by searching event sites, categorizing results, and generating a planning document

import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with comprehensive search for Tatar poet 'Moabit Däftäre'...") print("Target: Identify Tatar poet imprisoned in Berlin during WWII and poetry preserver/newspaper distributor") print("=" * 80) # Define targeted search queries for Moabit Däftäre and related information search_queries = [ 'Moabit Däftäre Tatar poet Berlin prison World War II', 'Tatar poetry preserved Berlin prison WWII', 'André Timmermans Tatar literature', 'banned newspaper Berlin prison Tatar poet distributor', 'Moabit Notebooks Tatar writer imprisoned Berlin', 'Tatar poet Berlin Moabit prison Second World War', 'André Timmermans preserved Tatar poetry Berlin', 'Moabit Däftäre Tatar literature Republic of Tatarstan', 'Berlin prison Tatar poet WWII André Timmermans newspaper', 'Tatar writer Moabit prison notebooks preserved poetry' ] print(f"Starting comprehensive search with {len(search_queries)} targeted queries...") print("Focus: Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet, André Timmermans, preserved poetry, banned newspaper") print("=" * 80) # Store all search results for analysis all_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Perform searches with different targeted queries for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 70) # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10, # Get sufficient results for comprehensive analysis "type": "search" } try: # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results for search {i}") successful_searches += 1 # Process and display key results for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\nResult {j}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Link: {link}") print(f"Snippet: {snippet}") # Store result with search context all_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet }) # Highlight potentially relevant results combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}" key_indicators = ['moabit', 'däftäre', 'tatar', 'andré timmermans', 'berlin', 'prison', 'wwii', 'world war', 'poetry', 'poet', 'preserved', 'newspaper', 'banned'] matching_indicators = [] for term in key_indicators: if term in combined_text: matching_indicators.append(term) if len(matching_indicators) >= 3: print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") # import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json from datetime import datetime import time # Since SerpAPI quota is exhausted, let's use direct web scraping with requests + BeautifulSoup # to search for information about Moabit Däftäre, the Tatar poet, and André Timmermans print("SerpAPI quota exhausted - switching to direct web scraping approach...") print("Target: Identify Tatar poet who wrote 'Moabit Däftäre' and André Timmermans' role") print("Strategy: Direct web scraping of search engines and relevant sites") print("=" * 80) # Set up headers to mimic a real browser headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1', } # Define search queries for direct web scraping search_queries = [ 'Moabit Däftäre Tatar poet Berlin prison World War II', 'André Timmermans Tatar literature preserved poetry', 'Moabit Notebooks Tatar writer imprisoned Berlin WWII', 'banned newspaper Berlin prison Tatar poet distributor André Timmermans', 'Tatar poetry Berlin Moabit prison Second World War preserved' ] print(f"Starting direct web scraping with {len(search_queries)} search queries...") print("Focus: Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet identification, André Timmermans, poetry preservation") print("=" * 80) # Store all scraped results all_scraped_results = [] successful_scrapes = 0 failed_scrapes = 0 # Function to scrape Google search results def scrape_google_search(query, max_results=10): """Scrape Google search results for a given query""" try: # Encode the query for URL encoded_query = query.replace(' ', '+') search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}" print(f"Scraping: {search_url}") # Make request to Google response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() # Parse the HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract search results results = [] # Find search result containers (Google's structure may vary) search_containers = soup.find_all('div', class_=['g', 'tF2Cxc', 'MjjYud']) for i, container in enumerate(search_containers[:max_results], 1): try: # Extract title title_elem = container.find(['h3', 'a']) title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else 'No title' # Extract link link_elem = container.find('a') link = link_elem.get('href', 'No link') if link_elem else 'No link' # Extract snippet/description snippet_elem = container.find(['span', 'div'], class_=['st', 'VwiC3b', 'yXK7lf']) if not snippet_elem: # Try alternative selectors for snippet snippet_elem = container.find('div', {'data-sncf': '1'}) if not snippet_elem: snippet_elem = container.find('span') snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else 'No snippet' # Clean up the link if it's a Google redirect if link.startswith('/url?q='): link = link.split('/url?q=')[1].split('&')[0] result = { 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'result_number': i } results.append(result) except Exception as e: print(f"Error extracting result {i}: {str(e)}") continue return results except Exception as e: print(f"Error scraping Google search: {str(e)}") return [] # Perform web scraping for each query for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nScraping Search {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 70) try: # Scrape Google search results scraped_results = scrape_google_search(query, max_results=8) if scraped_results: print(f"Successfully scraped {len(scraped_results)} results for query {i}") successful_scrapes += 1 # Process and display results for result in scraped_results: title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\nResult {result['result_number']}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Link: {link}") print(f"Snippet: {snippet}") # Store result with search context all_scraped_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': result['result_number'], 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'scrape_method': 'google_direct' }) # Analyze relevance combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}" key_indicators = ['moabit', 'däftäre', 'tatar', 'andré timmermans', 'berlin', 'prison', 'wwii', 'world war', 'poetry', 'poet', 'preserved', 'newspaper', 'banned'] matching_indicators = [] for term in key_indicators: if term in combined_text: matching_indicators.append(term) if len(matching_indicators) >= 3: print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") # import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json from datetime import datetime import time # Since SerpAPI quota is exhausted, let's use direct web scraping with requests + BeautifulSoup # to search for information about Moabit Däftäre, the Tatar poet, and André Timmermans print("SerpAPI quota exhausted - switching to direct web scraping approach...") print("Target: Identify Tatar poet who wrote 'Moabit Däftäre' and André Timmermans' role") print("Strategy: Direct web scraping of search engines and relevant sites") print("=" * 80) # Set up headers to mimic a real browser headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1', } # Define search queries for direct web scraping search_queries = [ 'Moabit Däftäre Tatar poet Berlin prison World War II', 'André Timmermans Tatar literature preserved poetry', 'Moabit Notebooks Tatar writer imprisoned Berlin WWII', 'banned newspaper Berlin prison Tatar poet distributor André Timmermans', 'Tatar poetry Berlin Moabit prison Second World War preserved' ] print(f"Starting direct web scraping with {len(search_queries)} search queries...") print("Focus: Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet identification, André Timmermans, poetry preservation") print("=" * 80) # Store all scraped results all_scraped_results = [] successful_scrapes = 0 failed_scrapes = 0 # Function to scrape Google search results def scrape_google_search(query, max_results=10): """Scrape Google search results for a given query""" try: # Encode the query for URL encoded_query = query.replace(' ', '+') search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}" print(f"Scraping: {search_url}") # Make request to Google response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() # Parse the HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract search results results = [] # Find search result containers (Google's structure may vary) search_containers = soup.find_all('div', class_=['g', 'tF2Cxc', 'MjjYud']) for i, container in enumerate(search_containers[:max_results], 1): try: # Extract title title_elem = container.find(['h3', 'a']) title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else 'No title' # Extract link link_elem = container.find('a') link = link_elem.get('href', 'No link') if link_elem else 'No link' # Extract snippet/description snippet_elem = container.find(['span', 'div'], class_=['st', 'VwiC3b', 'yXK7lf']) if not snippet_elem: # Try alternative selectors for snippet snippet_elem = container.find('div', {'data-sncf': '1'}) if not snippet_elem: snippet_elem = container.find('span') snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else 'No snippet' # Clean up the link if it's a Google redirect if link.startswith('/url?q='): link = link.split('/url?q=')[1].split('&')[0] result = { 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'result_number': i } results.append(result) except Exception as e: print(f"Error extracting result {i}: {str(e)}") continue return results except Exception as e: print(f"Error scraping Google search: {str(e)}") return [] # Perform web scraping for each query for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nScraping Search {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 70) try: # Scrape Google search results scraped_results = scrape_google_search(query, max_results=8) if scraped_results: print(f"Successfully scraped {len(scraped_results)} results for query {i}") successful_scrapes += 1 # Process and display results for result in scraped_results: title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\nResult {result['result_number']}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Link: {link}") print(f"Snippet: {snippet}") # Store result with search context all_scraped_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': result['result_number'], 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'scrape_method': 'google_direct' }) # Analyze relevance combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}" key_indicators = ['moabit', 'däftäre', 'tatar', 'andré timmermans', 'berlin', 'prison', 'wwii', 'world war', 'poetry', 'poet', 'preserved', 'newspaper', 'banned'] matching_indicators = [] for term in key_indicators: if term in combined_text: matching_indicators.append(term) if len(matching_indicators) >= 3: print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") # Check for specific key terms if 'moabit däftäre' in combined_text or 'moabit notebooks' in combined_text: print(f"📖 EXACT WORK MATCH: Contains Moabit Däftäre/Notebooks reference") if 'andré timmermans' in combined_text: print(f"👤 KEY PERSON: Contains André Timmermans reference") if 'tatar' in combined_text and ('poet' in combined_text or 'writer' in combined_text): print(f"🎭 AUTHOR MATCH: Contains Tatar poet/writer reference") if 'preserved' in combined_text or 'saved' in combined_text: print(f"📚 PRESERVATION: Contains preservation reference") if 'newspaper' in combined_text and 'banned' in combined_text: print(f"📰 BANNED MEDIA: Contains banned newspaper reference") elif len(matching_indicators) >= 1: print(f"📝 POTENTIALLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") print("-" * 40) else: print(f"No results scraped for query {i}: '{query}'") failed_scrapes += 1 all_scraped_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': 0, 'title': 'No results scraped', 'link': 'N/A', 'snippet': 'No results found via web scraping', 'scrape_method': 'google_direct' }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error during scraping {i}: {str(e)}") failed_scrapes += 1 continue # Add delay between requests to be respectful time.sleep(2) print("\n" + "=" * 80) # Save comprehensive scraping results to workspace timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") results_file = f"workspace/moabit_daftare_web_scraping_results_{timestamp}.json" with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'scraping_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'scraping_purpose': 'Identify Tatar poet who wrote Moabit Däftäre and André Timmermans role in preservation', 'scraping_method': 'Direct Google web scraping with requests + BeautifulSoup', 'search_focus': 'Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet, Berlin prison WWII, André Timmermans, preserved poetry, banned newspaper', 'total_queries': len(search_queries), 'successful_scrapes': successful_scrapes, 'failed_scrapes': failed_scrapes, 'total_results': len(all_scraped_results), 'queries_executed': search_queries, 'all_scraped_results': all_scraped_results }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n\n📊 WEB SCRAPING SUMMARY:") print(f"Total queries scraped: {len(search_queries)}") print(f"Successful scrapes: {successful_scrapes}") print(f"Failed scrapes: {failed_scrapes}") print(f"Total results collected: {len(all_scraped_results)}") print(f"Scraping results saved to: {results_file}") # Python Code python
import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json from datetime import datetime import time import urllib.parse # Fix the headers variable scope issue and implement proper web scraping # for Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet, and André Timmermans research print("Fixing web scraping approach for Moabit Däftäre research...") print("Target: Identify Tatar poet who wrote 'Moabit Däftäre' and André Timmermans' role") print("Strategy: Direct web scraping with proper variable scoping and error handling") print("=" * 80) # Function to scrape Google search results with proper headers definition def scrape_google_search(query, max_results=8): """Scrape Google search results for a given query with proper headers""" # Define headers inside the function to avoid scoping issues headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36', 'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8', 'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5', 'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate', 'Connection': 'keep-alive', 'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1', } try: # Encode the query for URL encoded_query = urllib.parse.quote_plus(query) search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={encoded_query}&num={max_results}" print(f"Scraping: {search_url}") # Make request to Google response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=15) response.raise_for_status() print(f"Response status: {response.status_code}") # Parse the HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract search results results = [] # Find search result containers (try multiple selectors) search_containers = soup.find_all('div', class_=['g', 'tF2Cxc', 'MjjYud', 'Gx5Zad']) print(f"Found {len(search_containers)} potential result containers") for i, container in enumerate(search_containers[:max_results], 1): try: # Extract title - try multiple selectors title_elem = container.find('h3') if not title_elem: title_elem = container.find('a') title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else f'Result {i} - No title' # Extract link link_elem = container.find('a') link = link_elem.get('href', 'No link') if link_elem else 'No link' # Clean up the link if it's a Google redirect if link.startswith('/url?q='): link = urllib.parse.unquote(link.split('/url?q=')[1].split('&')[0]) elif link.startswith('/search?'): link = 'Google internal link' # Extract snippet/description - try multiple selectors snippet_elem = container.find('span', class_=['st', 'VwiC3b', 'yXK7lf', 'hgKElc']) if not snippet_elem: snippet_elem = container.find('div', {'data-sncf': '1'}) if not snippet_elem: # Try to find any text content in the container text_content = container.get_text().strip() # Take first 200 characters as snippet snippet = text_content[:200] + '...' if len(text_content) > 200 else text_content else: snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() # Only include results with meaningful content if title and title != f'Result {i} - No title' and len(snippet) > 10: result = { 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'result_number': i } results.append(result) print(f"Extracted result {i}: {title[:50]}...") except Exception as e: print(f"Error extracting result {i}: {str(e)}") continue print(f"Successfully extracted {len(results)} valid results") return results except Exception as e: print(f"Error scraping Google search: {str(e)}") return [] # Define search queries for Moabit Däftäre research search_queries = [ 'Moabit Däftäre Tatar poet Berlin prison World War II', 'André Timmermans Tatar literature preserved poetry', 'Moabit Notebooks Tatar writer imprisoned Berlin WWII', 'banned newspaper Berlin prison Tatar poet distributor André Timmermans', 'Tatar poetry Berlin Moabit prison Second World War preserved', 'Moabit Däftäre Musa Cälil Tatar poet Berlin', 'André Timmermans preserved Tatar poetry Republic Tatarstan' ] print(f"Starting web scraping with {len(search_queries)} search queries...") print("Focus: Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet identification, André Timmermans, poetry preservation") print("=" * 80) # Store all scraped results all_scraped_results = [] successful_scrapes = 0 failed_scrapes = 0 # Perform web scraping for each query for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nScraping Search {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 70) try: # Scrape Google search results scraped_results = scrape_google_search(query, max_results=6) if scraped_results: print(f"Successfully scraped {len(scraped_results)} results for query {i}") successful_scrapes += 1 # Process and display results for result in scraped_results: title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\nResult {result['result_number']}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Link: {link}") print(f"Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...") # Truncate for display # Store result with search context all_scraped_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': result['result_number'], 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'scrape_method': 'google_direct_fixed' }) # Analyze relevance with key indicators combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}" key_indicators = ['moabit', 'däftäre', 'tatar', 'andré timmermans', 'musa', 'cälil', 'berlin', 'prison', 'wwii', 'world war', 'poetry', 'poet', 'preserved', 'newspaper', 'banned'] matching_indicators = [] for term in key_indicators: if term in combined_text: matching_indicators.append(term) if len(matching_indicators) >= 3: print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") # Check for specific key terms if 'moabit däftäre' in combined_text or 'moabit notebooks' in combined_text: print(f"📖 EXACT WORK MATCH: Contains Moabit Däftäre/Notebooks reference") if 'andré timmermans' in combined_text: print(f"👤 KEY PERSON: Contains André Timmermans reference") if 'musa' in combined_text and ('cälil' in combined_text or 'jalil' in combined_text): print(f"🎭 POET NAME: Contains Musa Cälil/Jalil reference") if 'tatar' in combined_text and (('poet' in combined_text) or ('writer' in combined_text)): print(f"🎭 AUTHOR MATCH: Contains Tatar poet/writer reference") if 'preserved' in combined_text or 'saved' in combined_text: print(f"📚 PRESERVATION: Contains preservation reference") if 'newspaper' in combined_text and 'banned' in combined_text: print(f"📰 BANNED MEDIA: Contains banned newspaper reference") elif len(matching_indicators) >= 1: print(f"📝 POTENTIALLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") print("-" * 40) else: print(f"No results scraped for query {i}: '{query}'") failed_scrapes += 1 all_scraped_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': 0, 'title': 'No results scraped', 'link': 'N/A', 'snippet': 'No results found via web scraping', 'scrape_method': 'google_direct_fixed' }) except Exception as e: print(f"Error during scraping {i}: {str(e)}") failed_scrapes += 1 continue # Add delay between requests to be respectful time.sleep(3) print("\n" + "=" * 80) # Save comprehensive scraping results to workspace timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") results_file = f"workspace/moabit_daftare_fixed_scraping_results_{timestamp}.json" with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'scraping_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'scraping_purpose': 'Identify Tatar poet who wrote Moabit Däftäre and André Timmermans role in preservation', 'scraping_method': 'Fixed Google web scraping with proper headers and error handling', 'search_focus': 'Moabit Däftäre, Tatar poet (Musa Cälil), Berlin prison WWII, André Timmermans, preserved poetry, banned newspaper', 'total_queries': len(search_queries), 'successful_scrapes': successful_scrapes, 'failed_scrapes': failed_scrapes, 'total_results': len(all_scraped_results), 'queries_executed': search_queries, 'all_scraped_results': all_scraped_results }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n\n📊 FIXED WEB SCRAPING SUMMARY:") print(f"Total queries scraped: {len(search_queries)}") print(f"Successful scrapes: {successful_scrapes}") print(f"Failed scrapes: {failed_scrapes}") print(f"Total results collected: {len(all_scraped_results)}") print(f"Scraping results saved to: {results_file}") # Quick analysis for immediate insights print("\n\n🔍 ANALYSIS FOR MOABIT DÄFTÄRE AND TATAR POET:") print("=" * 60) # Categorize results by relevance moabit_results = [] tatar_poet_results = [] andre_timmermans_results = [] preservation_results = [] newspaper_results = [] berlin_prison_results = [] musa_results = [] for result in all_scraped_results: if result['title'] == 'No results scraped': continue title_lower = result['title'].lower() snippet_lower = result['snippet'].lower() combined = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}" # Categorize by relevance to our specific search if 'moabit' in combined and ('däftäre' in combined or 'notebooks' in combined): moabit_results.append(result) if 'tatar' in combined and ('poet' in combined or 'writer' in combined or 'poetry' in combined): tatar_poet_results.append(result) if 'andré timmermans' in combined or 'andre timmermans' in combined: andre_timmermans_results.append(result) if any(term in combined for term in ['preserved', 'preservation', 'saved', 'rescued', 'collected']): preservation_results.append(result) if 'newspaper' in combined and ('banned' in combined or 'underground' in combined or 'illegal' in combined): newspaper_results.append(result) if 'berlin' in combined and ('prison' in combined or 'jail' in combined or 'imprisoned' in combined): berlin_prison_results.append(result) if 'musa' in combined and ('cälil' in combined or 'jalil' in combined): musa_results.append(result) print(f"\n📋 CATEGORIZATION RESULTS:") print(f"Results mentioning Moabit Däftäre/Notebooks: {len(moabit_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning Tatar poet/poetry: {len(tatar_poet_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning André Timmermans: {len(andre_timmermans_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning preservation: {len(preservation_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning banned newspaper: {len(newspaper_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning Berlin prison: {len(berlin_prison_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning Musa Cälil/Jalil: {len(musa_results)}") # Display most promising results if moabit_results: print("\n\n🎯 MOABIT DÄFTÄRE MATCHES:") print("=" * 40) for i, result in enumerate(moabit_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3 print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:200]}...") print(f" Search #{result['search_number']}, Result #{result['result_number']}") else: print("\n⚠️ No direct Moabit Däftäre matches found") if musa_results: print("\n\n🎭 MUSA CÄLIL/JALIL MATCHES:") print("=" * 35) for i, result in enumerate(musa_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3 print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:200]}...") else: print("\n⚠️ No Musa Cälil/Jalil matches found") if andre_timmermans_results: print("\n\n👤 ANDRÉ TIMMERMANS MATCHES:") print("=" * 35) for i, result in enumerate(andre_timmermans_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3 print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:200]}...") else: print("\n⚠️ No André Timmermans matches found") # Show most relevant overall results print("\n\n🔍 MOST RELEVANT OVERALL RESULTS:") print("=" * 40) # Find results with multiple key indicators highly_relevant = [] for result in all_scraped_results: if result['title'] == 'No results scraped': continue combined_text = f"{result['title'].lower()} {result['snippet'].lower()}" key_indicators = ['moabit', 'däftäre', 'tatar', 'andré timmermans', 'musa', 'cälil', 'berlin', 'prison', 'wwii', 'poetry', 'poet', 'preserved', 'newspaper'] matching_count = sum(1 for term in key_indicators if term in combined_text) if matching_count >= 2: # Lower threshold to capture more results highly_relevant.append((result, matching_count)) # Sort by relevance score highly_relevant.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True) if highly_relevant: for i, (result, score) in enumerate(highly_relevant[:5], 1): # Show top 5 print(f"\n{i}. [Score: {score}] {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:250]}...") else: print("\nNo highly relevant results found with multiple key indicators") print(f"\n\n📁 Results saved to: {results_file}") print("🎯 Goal: Extract specific names and connections from scraped content") print("🔍 Focus: Identify the Tatar poet's name (likely Musa Cälil) and André Timmermans' preservation role") print("\n🏁 Fixed web scraping phase complete - ready for detailed content analysis!")

### Development Step 7: Identify Berlin Football Club Winning 1984 DDR-Pokal and Its October 2, 1985 European Match

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify the Berlin-based football club that won the last East German Cup in 1984. Search for keywords including 'East German Cup 1984 winner Berlin football club', 'DDR-Pokal 1984 final Berlin team', 'last East German Cup 1984 champion', and 'GDR Cup 1984 Berlin football'. Focus on identifying which Berlin club won this final East German Cup tournament and gather information about their European competition participation in the 1985-86 season, particularly any matches on 2 October 1985.

**Use Cases**:
- Sports historians automating the retrieval of archived match reports and statistics for museum exhibitions on East German football
- Investigative sports journalists verifying specific game dates, opponents, and venues to fact-check feature articles on BFC Dynamo’s European campaigns
- Football fan sites populating their club history pages with accurate details from the 1985-86 UEFA Cup Winners’ Cup using targeted web searches
- Documentary researchers compiling precise timelines and contextual snippets for a film on DDR-era football through multi-query API extraction
- Academic sports scientists aggregating performance data of East German clubs in European competitions for statistical trend analysis
- Data engineers building a structured historical sports database by systematically querying and filtering online sources for exact match information
- Educators designing interactive quizzes and lesson plans on German football history, automatically sourcing validated match outcomes and dates
- Mobile app developers integrating a dynamic timeline feature that auto-loads historical match events (e.g., 2 October 1985) for fan engagement tools

```
import os
import requests
import json
from datetime import datetime

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
print("API key found, proceeding with targeted search for BFC Dynamo's 2 October 1985 European match...")
print("Based on previous analysis: BFC Dynamo was Berlin finalist in 1984 East German Cup (lost to Dresden)")
print("Target: Find specific European competition match on 2 October 1985")
print("=" * 80)

# Define targeted search queries for BFC Dynamo's 2 October 1985 European match
search_queries = [
'BFC Dynamo "2 October 1985" European competition match',
'Berliner FC Dynamo "October 2 1985" UEFA Cup Winners Cup',
'BFC Dynamo European match "2.10.1985" opponent venue',
'Berliner FC Dynamo "2nd October 1985" European football',
'BFC Dynamo 1985-86 European season "October 2" match report',
'East German BFC Dynamo "2 October 1985" European Cup',
'Dynamo Berlin "2.10.85" European competition result',
'BFC Dynamo 1985 European matches October 2nd opponent'
]

print(f"Starting targeted search with {len(search_queries)} specific queries...")
print("Focus: BFC Dynamo European match on exactly 2 October 1985")
print("=" * 80)

# Store all search results for analysis
all_results = []
successful_searches = 0
failed_searches = 0

# Perform searches with different targeted queries
for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}")
print("-" * 70)

# Prepare API request parameters
params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 10, # Get sufficient results for comprehensive analysis
"type": "search"
}

try:
# Make API request to SerpAPI
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()

if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results for search {i}")
successful_searches += 1

# Process and display key results
for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f"\nResult {j}:")
print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"Link: {link}")
print(f"Snippet: {snippet}")

# Store result with search context
all_results.append({
'search_number': i,
'query_text': query,
'result_number': j,
'title': title,
'link': link,
'snippet': snippet
})

# Highlight potentially relevant results
combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}"
key_indicators = ['bfc dynamo', 'berliner fc dynamo', '2 october', 'october 2', '2.10.1985', 'european', 'uefa', 'cup winners']
matching_indicators = []
for term in key_indicators:
if term in combined_text:
matching_indicators.append(term)

if len(matching_indicators) >= 2:
print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}")

# Check for specific match details
if '2 october' in combined_text or 'october 2' in combined_text or '2.10.1985' in combined_text:
print(f"🗓️ EXACT DATE MATCH: Contains 2 October 1985 reference")
if 'opponent' in combined_text or 'vs' in combined_text or 'against' in combined_text:
print(f"⚽ MATCH DETAILS: Contains opponent information")
if 'venue' in combined_text or 'stadium' in combined_text:
print(f"🏟️ VENUE INFO: Contains stadium/venue details")

print("-" * 40)
else:
print(f"No organic results found for search {i}: '{query}'")
failed_searches += 1
all_results.append({
'search_number': i,
'query_text': query,
'result_number': 0,
'title': 'No results',
'link': 'N/A',
'snippet': 'No results found for this query'
})

else:
print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
failed_searches += 1

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}")
failed_searches += 1
continue

print("\n" + "=" * 80)

# Save comprehensive search results to workspace
timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
results_file = f"workspace/bfc_dynamo_2_october_1985_search_results_{timestamp}.json"

with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump({
'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
'search_purpose': 'BFC Dynamo European match on 2 October 1985 - targeted search',
'background_context': 'BFC Dynamo was Berlin finalist in 1984 East German Cup (lost to Dresden), regular European participant',
'total_queries': len(search_queries),
'successful_searches': successful_searches,
'failed_searches': failed_searches,
'total_results': len(all_results),
'queries_executed': search_queries,
'results': all_results
}, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"\n\n📊 TARGETED SEARCH SUMMARY:")
print(f"Total targeted queries executed: {len(search_queries)}")
print(f"Successful searches: {successful_searches}")
print(f"Failed searches: {failed_searches}")
print(f"Total results collected: {len(all_results)}")
print(f"Search results saved to: {results_file}")

# Quick analysis for immediate insights
print("\n\n🔍 QUICK ANALYSIS FOR 2 OCTOBER 1985 MATCH:")
print("=" * 60)

# Look for results specifically mentioning the exact date
exact_date_results = []
european_match_results = []
bfc_dynamo_results = []

for result in all_results:
if result['title'] == 'No results':
continue

title_lower = result['title'].lower()
snippet_lower = result['snippet'].lower()
combined = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}"

# Categorize by relevance to our specific search
if '2 october' in combined or 'october 2' in combined or '2.10.1985' in combined or '2.10.85' in combined:
exact_date_results.append(result)

if any(term in combined for term in ['european', 'uefa', 'cup winners', 'european cup']) and ('bfc dynamo' in combined or 'berliner fc dynamo' in combined):
european_match_results.append(result)

if 'bfc dynamo' in combined or 'berliner fc dynamo' in combined:
bfc_dynamo_results.append(result)

print(f"\n📋 QUICK CATEGORIZATION:")
print(f"Results with exact date (2 October 1985): {len(exact_date_results)}")
print(f"Results with BFC Dynamo European matches: {len(european_match_results)}")
print(f"Results mentioning BFC Dynamo: {len(bfc_dynamo_results)}")

# Display most promising results
if exact_date_results:
print("\n\n🎯 EXACT DATE MATCHES (2 October 1985):")
print("=" * 50)
for i, result in enumerate(exact_date_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3
print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}")
print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}")
print(f" Link: {result['link']}")
print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}")
print(f" Search #{result['search_number']}, Result #{result['result_number']}")
else:
print("\n⚠️ No exact date matches found for 2 October 1985")

if european_match_results:
print("\n\n🌍 BFC DYNAMO EUROPEAN COMPETITION RESULTS:")
print("=" * 50)
for i, result in enumerate(european_match_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3
print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}")
print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}")
print(f" Link: {result['link']}")
print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}")
else:
print("\n⚠️ No specific BFC Dynamo European match results found")

print(f"\n\n📁 Next step: Analyze detailed results in {results_file}")
print("🎯 Goal: Identify BFC Dynamo's specific European match on 2 October 1985")
print("🔍 Focus: Match opponent, venue, competition, and result details")
print("\n🏁 Targeted search phase complete - ready for detailed analysis!")
```

```
break

if i <= 10:

if i <= 10:

if comp_term in result_combined_text:
has_european_cup = True
break

european_cup_results.append(result)
if i <= 10:

# Check for match details (score, goals, etc.)

for detail_term in detail_terms:

has_match_details = True
```

import os import requests import json from datetime import datetime # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with search for André Timmermans banned newspaper...") print("Target: Find the exact name of the banned newspaper André Timmermans distributed during WWII in Berlin") print("Focus: Historical records of resistance newspaper operations in Berlin prison during wartime") print("=" * 80) # Define targeted search queries for André Timmermans banned newspaper search_queries = [ 'André Timmermans banned newspaper Berlin WWII', 'André Timmermans distributed newspaper prison Berlin World War II', 'banned newspaper Berlin World War II Timmermans', 'underground newspaper distribution Berlin prison WWII André Timmermans', 'André Timmermans resistance newspaper Berlin wartime', 'clandestine newspaper Berlin prison World War 2 Timmermans', 'André Timmermans imprisoned Berlin newspaper distribution WWII', 'banned underground newspaper André Timmermans Berlin 1940s' ] print(f"Starting comprehensive search with {len(search_queries)} targeted queries...") print("Focus: Identifying the exact name of the banned newspaper distributed by André Timmermans") print("=" * 80) # Store all search results for analysis all_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Perform searches with different targeted queries for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 70) # Prepare API request parameters params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10, # Get sufficient results for comprehensive analysis "type": "search" } try: # Make API request to SerpAPI response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results for search {i}") successful_searches += 1 # Process and display key results for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\nResult {j}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Link: {link}") print(f"Snippet: {snippet}") # Store result with search context all_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet }) # Highlight potentially relevant results combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}" key_indicators = ['andré timmermans', 'timmermans', 'banned newspaper', 'underground newspaper', 'resistance newspaper', 'berlin', 'wwii', 'world war', 'prison', 'distributed'] matching_indicators = [] for term in key_indicators: if term in combined_text: matching_indicators.append(term) if len(matching_indicators) >= 3: print(f"🎯 HIGHLY RELEVANT - Contains: {', '.join(matching_indicators)}") # Check for specific newspaper names or titles newspaper_indicators = ['newspaper', 'journal', 'bulletin', 'publication', 'leaflet', 'pamphlet'] for indicator in newspaper_indicators: if indicator in combined_text: print(f"📰 NEWSPAPER REFERENCE: Contains '{indicator}'") break # Check for resistance/underground context if 'resistance' in combined_text or 'underground' in combined_text or 'clandestine' in combined_text: print(f"🕵️ RESISTANCE CONTEXT: Contains underground/resistance references") # Check for Berlin prison context if 'berlin' in combined_text and ('prison' in combined_text or 'imprisoned' in combined_text): print(f"🏢 BERLIN PRISON CONTEXT: Contains Berlin prison references") print("-" * 40) else: print(f"No organic results found for search {i}: '{query}'") failed_searches += 1 all_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query_text': query, 'result_number': 0, 'title': 'No results', 'link': 'N/A', 'snippet': 'No results found for this query' }) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}") failed_searches += 1 continue print("\n" + "=" * 80) # Save comprehensive search results to workspace timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") results_file = f"workspace/andre_timmermans_banned_newspaper_search_results_{timestamp}.json" with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'search_purpose': 'André Timmermans banned newspaper identification - WWII Berlin resistance', 'search_focus': 'Find exact name of banned newspaper distributed by André Timmermans in Berlin during WWII', 'total_queries': len(search_queries), 'successful_searches': successful_searches, 'failed_searches': failed_searches, 'total_results': len(all_results), 'queries_executed': search_queries, 'all_search_results': all_results }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n\n📊 COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH SUMMARY:") print(f"Total targeted queries executed: {len(search_queries)}") print(f"Successful searches: {successful_searches}") print(f"Failed searches: {failed_searches}") print(f"Total results collected: {len(all_results)}") print(f"Search results saved to: {results_file}") # Quick analysis for immediate insights print("\n\n🔍 QUICK ANALYSIS FOR ANDRÉ TIMMERMANS BANNED NEWSPAPER:") print("=" * 65) # Look for results specifically mentioning André Timmermans and newspapers timmermans_results = [] newspaper_results = [] resistance_results = [] berlin_prison_results = [] for result in all_results: if result['title'] == 'No results': continue title_lower = result['title'].lower() snippet_lower = result['snippet'].lower() combined = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower}" # Categorize by relevance to our specific search if 'andré timmermans' in combined or 'timmermans' in combined: timmermans_results.append(result) if 'newspaper' in combined or 'journal' in combined or 'publication' in combined or 'bulletin' in combined: newspaper_results.append(result) if 'resistance' in combined or 'underground' in combined or 'clandestine' in combined: resistance_results.append(result) if 'berlin' in combined and ('prison' in combined or 'imprisoned' in combined): berlin_prison_results.append(result) print(f"\n📋 CATEGORIZATION RESULTS:") print(f"Results mentioning André Timmermans: {len(timmermans_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning newspapers/publications: {len(newspaper_results)}") print(f"Results with resistance/underground context: {len(resistance_results)}") print(f"Results with Berlin prison context: {len(berlin_prison_results)}") # Display most promising results if timmermans_results: print("\n\n🎯 ANDRÉ TIMMERMANS SPECIFIC RESULTS:") print("=" * 45) for i, result in enumerate(timmermans_results[:5], 1): # Show top 5 print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}") print(f" Search #{result['search_number']}, Result #{result['result_number']}") # Check for newspaper name mentions in snippet snippet_text = result['snippet'].lower() if 'newspaper' in snippet_text: print(f" 📰 CONTAINS NEWSPAPER REFERENCE") if 'banned' in snippet_text: print(f" 🚫 CONTAINS BANNED REFERENCE") if 'distributed' in snippet_text or 'distribution' in snippet_text: print(f" 📤 CONTAINS DISTRIBUTION REFERENCE") else: print("\n⚠️ No specific André Timmermans results found") if resistance_results: print("\n\n🕵️ RESISTANCE/UNDERGROUND NEWSPAPER RESULTS:") print("=" * 50) for i, result in enumerate(resistance_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3 print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}") else: print("\n⚠️ No resistance/underground newspaper results found") print(f"\n\n📁 Next step: Analyze detailed results in {results_file}") print("🎯 Goal: Identify the exact name of the banned newspaper André Timmermans distributed") print("🔍 Focus: Historical documentation, resistance archives, wartime records") print("\n🏁 Initial search phase complete - ready for detailed analysis!")

Categorize by relevance to our specific search if 'andré timmermans' in combined or 'timmermans' in combined: timmermans_results.append(result) if 'newspaper' in combined or 'journal' in combined or 'publication' in combined or 'bulletin' in combined: newspaper_results.append(result) if 'resistance' in combined or 'underground' in combined or 'clandestine' in combined: resistance_results.append(result) if 'berlin' in combined and ('prison' in combined or 'imprisoned' in combined): berlin_prison_results.append(result) print(f"\n📋 CATEGORIZATION RESULTS:") print(f"Results mentioning André Timmermans: {len(timmermans_results)}") print(f"Results mentioning newspapers/publications: {len(newspaper_results)}") print(f"Results with resistance/underground context: {len(resistance_results)}") print(f"Results with Berlin prison context: {len(berlin_prison_results)}") # Check for newspaper name mentions in snippet snippet_text = result['snippet'].lower() if 'newspaper' in snippet_text: print(f" 📰 CONTAINS NEWSPAPER REFERENCE") if 'banned' in snippet_text: print(f" 🚫 CONTAINS BANNED REFERENCE") if 'distributed' in snippet_text or 'distribution' in snippet_text: print(f" 📤 CONTAINS DISTRIBUTION REFERENCE") else: print("\n⚠️ No specific André Timmermans results found") if resistance_results: print("\n\n🕵️ RESISTANCE/UNDERGROUND NEWSPAPER RESULTS:") print("=" * 50) for i, result in enumerate(resistance_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3 print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" Query: {result['query_text']}") print(f" Link: {result['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet']}") else: print("\n⚠️ No resistance/underground newspaper results found") print(f"\n\n📁 Next step: Analyze detailed results in {results_file}") print("🎯 Goal: Identify the exact name of the banned newspaper André Timmermans distributed") print("🔍 Focus: Historical documentation, resistance archives, wartime records") print("\n🏁 Initial search phase complete - ready for detailed analysis!")

import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json from datetime import datetime import time # Since SerpAPI has run out of searches, let's try alternative approaches # First, let's check what we have in the workspace from the failed search print("Checking workspace for any existing search results...") if os.path.exists('workspace'): files = os.listdir('workspace') print(f"Files in workspace: {files}") # Look for the search results file that was created timmermans_files = [f for f in files if 'andre_timmermans_banned_newspaper_search_results_' in f] if timmermans_files: results_file = f'workspace/{timmermans_files[0]}' print(f"\nFound search results file: {results_file}") # Inspect the file structure first try: with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File structure - Keys: {list(data.keys())}") print(f"Search purpose: {data.get('search_purpose', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total results: {data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}") print(f"Successful searches: {data.get('successful_searches', 'N/A')}") if data.get('total_results', 0) == 0: print("\n❌ Confirmed: No search results obtained due to API quota exhaustion") except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading file: {e}") else: print("No workspace directory found") print("\n" + "="*80) print("ALTERNATIVE RESEARCH APPROACH - DIRECT WEB SCRAPING") print("="*80) print("Since SerpAPI quota is exhausted, attempting direct web scraping of historical sources...") # Try direct access to historical and biographical websites historical_sources = [ { 'name': 'Wikipedia - André Timmermans', 'url': 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/André_Timmermans', 'backup_url': 'https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/André_Timmermans' }, { 'name': 'Wikipedia - Belgian Resistance', 'url': 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgian_resistance', 'backup_url': None }, { 'name': 'Wikipedia - Underground Press WWII', 'url': 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Underground_press', 'backup_url': None } ] headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } scraping_results = [] for source in historical_sources: print(f"\n🔍 Attempting to scrape: {source['name']}") print(f"URL: {source['url']}") print("-" * 60) try: response = requests.get(source['url'], headers=headers, timeout=15) if response.status_code == 200: soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() # Get text content text = soup.get_text() lines = (line.strip() for line in text.splitlines()) chunks = (phrase.strip() for line in lines for phrase in line.split(" ")) clean_text = ' '.join(chunk for chunk in chunks if chunk) print(f"✅ Successfully scraped {len(clean_text)} characters") # Search for André Timmermans mentions text_lower = clean_text.lower() if 'andré timmermans' in text_lower or 'andre timmermans' in text_lower: print("🎯 FOUND ANDRÉ TIMMERMANS MENTION!") # Extract relevant paragraphs paragraphs = clean_text.split('.') relevant_paragraphs = [] for para in paragraphs: para_lower = para.lower() if ('andré timmermans' in para_lower or 'andre timmermans' in para_lower) or \ ('timmermans' in para_lower and ('newspaper' in para_lower or 'banned' in para_lower or 'prison' in para_lower)): relevant_paragraphs.append(para.strip()) if relevant_paragraphs: print(f"\n📰 RELEVANT CONTENT FOUND ({len(relevant_paragraphs)} paragraphs):") for i, para in enumerate(relevant_paragraphs[:5], 1): # Show first 5 print(f"\n{i}. {para}") scraping_results.append({ 'source': source['name'], 'url': source['url'], 'relevant_paragraphs': relevant_paragraphs, 'full_text_length': len(clean_text) }) else: print("📝 Timmermans mentioned but no newspaper-specific content found") else: print("❌ No André Timmermans mentions found") # Still check for general resistance newspaper information if 'resistance' in text_lower and 'newspaper' in text_lower and 'berlin' in text_lower: print("🕵️ Found general resistance newspaper information in Berlin context") # Extract resistance-related paragraphs paragraphs = clean_text.split('.') resistance_paragraphs = [] for para in paragraphs: para_lower = para.lower() if 'resistance' in para_lower and ('newspaper' in para_lower or 'publication' in para_lower) and 'berlin' in para_lower: resistance_paragraphs.append(para.strip()) if resistance_paragraphs: print(f"\n🔍 RESISTANCE NEWSPAPER CONTEXT ({len(resistance_paragraphs)} paragraphs):") for i, para in enumerate(resistance_paragraphs[:3], 1): print(f"\n{i}. {para}") elif response.status_code == 404 and source.get('backup_url'): print(f"⚠️ Main URL failed (404), trying backup: {source['backup_url']}") backup_response = requests.get(source['backup_url'], headers=headers, timeout=15) if backup_response.status_code == 200: print(f"✅ Backup URL successful") # Process backup response similar to above soup = BeautifulSoup(backup_response.content, 'html.parser') for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.decompose() text = soup.get_text() print(f"Scraped {len(text)} characters from backup URL") else: print(f"❌ Backup URL also failed: {backup_response.status_code}") else: print(f"❌ Failed to access: HTTP {response.status_code}") except requests.exceptions.Timeout: print("⏰ Request timed out") except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e: print(f"❌ Request error: {str(e)}") except Exception as e: print(f"❌ Unexpected error: {str(e)}") # Small delay between requests to be respectful time.sleep(2) print("\n" + "="*80) print("SCRAPING RESULTS ANALYSIS") print("="*80) if scraping_results: print(f"\n✅ Successfully found relevant information from {len(scraping_results)} sources") # Save scraping results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") scraping_file = f"workspace/andre_timmermans_scraping_results_{timestamp}.json" with open(scraping_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump({ 'scraping_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'scraping_purpose': 'Alternative research for André Timmermans banned newspaper after SerpAPI quota exhaustion', 'sources_attempted': len(historical_sources), 'successful_sources': len(scraping_results), 'results': scraping_results }, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"📄 Scraping results saved to: {scraping_file}") # Analyze the content for newspaper names print("\n🔍 ANALYZING SCRAPED CONTENT FOR BANNED NEWSPAPER NAMES:") print("-" * 60) all_paragraphs = [] for result in scraping_results: all_paragraphs.extend(result['relevant_paragraphs']) # Look for potential newspaper names newspaper_indicators = ['newspaper', 'journal', 'bulletin', 'publication', 'leaflet', 'pamphlet', 'gazette', 'herald'] banned_indicators = ['banned', 'prohibited', 'forbidden', 'illegal', 'underground', 'clandestine'] potential_newspapers = [] for para in all_paragraphs: para_lower = para.lower() if any(news_word in para_lower for news_word in newspaper_indicators) and \ any(ban_word in para_lower for ban_word in banned_indicators): potential_newspapers.append(para) if potential_newspapers: print(f"\n📰 POTENTIAL NEWSPAPER REFERENCES FOUND ({len(potential_newspapers)}):") for i, ref in enumerate(potential_newspapers, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {ref}") else: print("\n❌ No specific banned newspaper names identified in scraped content") else: print("\n❌ No relevant information found through direct web scraping") print("\n" + "="*80) print("RESEARCH STATUS AND NEXT STEPS") print("="*80) print("\n📊 CURRENT SITUATION:") print("• SerpAPI quota exhausted - no search results obtained") print("• Direct web scraping attempted on historical sources") print(f"• {len(scraping_results)} sources successfully scraped") print("\n🎯 FINDINGS SUMMARY:") if scraping_results: print("• Some historical content about André Timmermans or resistance found") print("• Content analysis completed for banned newspaper references") else: print("• No specific information about André Timmermans found in accessible sources") print("• May require specialized historical archives or academic databases") print("\n🔍 RECOMMENDED NEXT STEPS:") print("1. Wait for SerpAPI quota reset and retry targeted searches") print("2. Access specialized WWII resistance archives and databases") print("3. Contact historical research institutions or libraries") print("4. Search academic papers and dissertations on Belgian resistance") print("5. Check newspaper archives from the WWII period") print("\n📝 RESEARCH CHALLENGE:") print("André Timmermans and the specific banned newspaper he distributed") print("during WWII in Berlin may be documented in specialized historical") print("archives that are not readily accessible through general web searches.") print("This type of resistance activity documentation often requires") print("access to academic databases, museum archives, or government records.") print("\n🏁 ALTERNATIVE RESEARCH PHASE COMPLETED")

Look for potential newspaper names newspaper_indicators = ['newspaper', 'journal', 'bulletin', 'publication', 'leaflet', 'pamphlet', 'gazette', 'herald'] banned_indicators = ['banned', 'prohibited', 'forbidden', 'illegal', 'underground', 'clandestine'] potential_newspapers = [] for para in all_paragraphs: para_lower = para.lower() if any(news_word in para_lower for news_word in newspaper_indicators) and \ any(ban_word in para_lower for ban_word in banned_indicators): potential_newspapers.append(para) if potential_newspapers: print(f"\n📰 POTENTIAL NEWSPAPER REFERENCES FOUND ({len(potential_newspapers)}):") for i, ref in enumerate(potential_newspapers, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {ref}") else: print("\n❌ No specific banned newspaper names identified in scraped content") else: print("\n❌ No relevant information found through direct web scraping") print("\n" + "="*80) print("RESEARCH STATUS AND NEXT STEPS") print("="*80) print("\n📊 CURRENT SITUATION:") print("• SerpAPI quota exhausted - no search results obtained") print("• Direct web scraping attempted on historical sources") print(f"• {len(scraping_results)} sources successfully scraped") print("\n🎯 FINDINGS SUMMARY:") if scraping_results: print("• Some historical content about André Timmermans or resistance found") print("• Content analysis completed for banned newspaper references") else: print("• No specific information about André Timmermans found in accessible sources") print("• May require specialized historical archives or academic databases") print("\n🔍 RECOMMENDED NEXT STEPS:") print("1.
